is identical to Boggle. Search for words and type away. Only words 3 letters and up are considered, and you can't go over the same letter twice.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eControls\u003c/h3\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-controls\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Controls\" href=\"#controls\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eSpacebar\u003c/strong\u003e: Rotates the board clockwise. This does not alter the current tile distribution, but is very useful in getting a new perspective on the board.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eESC:\u003c/strong\u003e Pauses the game. The timer freezes, and tiles go blank until it is unpaused.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eBoard Generation\u003c/h3\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-board-generation\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Board Generation\" href=\"#board-generation\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eDepending on your game type, a board will be generated at random (no curated boards here, unlike other Boggle wannabe apps!) based on a probability chance for each letter. The probability of a given letter to appear on the board is the same as that of in a game of Scrabble. For example, out of the 100 tiles in a standard Scrabble game, \"E\" has 12 tiles, and \"Q\" has 1. Therefore, E has a 12% chance of appearing in a given tile, and Q has a 1% chance. This creates a natural distribution of letters that would be as similar as possible to a competitive Scrabble game.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eSummary Screen\u003c/h3\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-summary-screen\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Summary Screen\" 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eAt the end of each round, you will be shown a summary of your performance, including your rank letter, round score, badges earned, a list of possible words that you missed (in black) and words that you correctly guessed (in green) with their respective scores:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv align=\"center\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" Classification (Background Colors)\u003c/h3\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-board-classification-background-colors\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Board Classification (Background Colors)\" href=\"#board-classification-background-colors\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eWhat makes Woggy unique to other Boggle clones is its dynamic timer and scoring system. Why would we play for 3:00 minutes on a board that only has 10 words? When you start a board, the total possible score for it is calculated, and a board classification is assigned to it depending on how much potential there is on the board. For very closed boards, the timer is shrunk to as little as 15 seconds and the background turns \u003cstrong\u003ered\u003c/strong\u003e to indicate a sense of urgency. This type of board will more challenge your speed on finding the few words available. On the other hand, boards with huge score potentials have more exotic background colors, such as sky blue, purple, and green, and feature much longer times (up to 300 seconds!).\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThe background color gives you a hint on how to play: You will want to hurry up on the reddish boards and change your playstyle for more relaxed play on lighter-colored boards.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThe board's classification nickname is displayed in the End Screen, and it ranges from \u003ccode\u003eImpossible Board!\u003c/code\u003e all the way to \u003ccode\u003eGodlike Board!\u003c/code\u003e depending on its potential. There are currently 32 total categories where a board can fit into, each with its own unique timer and scoring parameters.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv align=\"center\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" file will be automatically be generated under the \u003cstrong\u003eScores\u003c/strong\u003e folder with the date on the title and a breakdown of the entire round. Useful for keeping track of high scores!\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eOptions\u003c/h3\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-options\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Options\" href=\"#options\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e-\u003cstrong\u003eTile Size\u003c/strong\u003e: This will resize the board tiles for better readability. Please be advised, since the game is still extremely early in development, I haven't yet tested all tile sizes to look good.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e-\u003cstrong\u003eWord Judge\u003c/strong\u003e: Turning this off will turn off the comments you get at the end of each round. For those who prefer a judgement-free Woggy experience!\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eAll options and latest preferences are automatically saved in \u003ccode\u003eSettings\\settings.json\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eScoring Rules\u003c/h2\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-scoring-rules\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Scoring Rules\" href=\"#scoring-rules\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eEach tile in Woggy scores the same amount as it does in an official Scrabble board * 10. For example, E = 10, F = 40, Q = 100, etc. In its pure form, the word \u003ccode\u003eSQUADS\u003c/code\u003e would be worth 160 points.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThe main difference in scoring is that longer words now have a much higher weight to them due to \u003cstrong\u003escore multipliers\u003c/strong\u003e. The longer the word, the higher the score multiplier (as opposed to a measly flat bonus the original Boggle grants). This is a great implementation for those who love to seek long words in the board, and it properly compensates players who have the skill required to find them. Here is how much each word is affected by its length:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv align=\"center\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cmarkdown-accessiblity-table\u003e\u003ctable\u003e\n\u003cthead\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003cth\u003eWord letters\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e2x\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e8 letters\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e2.5x\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e9 letters\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e3x\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e10 letters\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e4x\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e11 letters\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e5x\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e12 letters\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e6x\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e13 letters\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e7x\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e14 letters\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e8x\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e15 letters\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e10x\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e16 letters\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e12x\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003c/tbody\u003e\n\u003c/table\u003e\u003c/markdown-accessiblity-table\u003e\n\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eWith this scoring logic, \u003ccode\u003eSQUADS\u003c/code\u003e will be worth 280 points, instead of its base 160. While this scoring system might seem a bit overboard, keep in mind that words longer than 9 or 10 are quite rare to find. In the rare occassion that one does exist, one will be properly compensated for finding it.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eRank Determination\u003c/h3\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-rank-determination\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Rank Determination\" href=\"#rank-determination\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eDepending on your performance, you will be shown a rank letter in your end screen. These range from \u003ccode\u003eF-\u003c/code\u003e all the way to a legendary \u003ccode\u003eSS\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThis score is calculated by several factors, but at its core, it is based on what percentage of the potential score you earned in a given board. For example, only getting a 5% score will net you an \u003ccode\u003eF-\u003c/code\u003e, but netting 45% will get you a solid \u003ccode\u003eA\u003c/code\u003e. There are a few more factors to consider, though. \"Extreme\" boards (very closed or very open) have a handicap to offset scores in an effort to make them more balanced. This means that in order to get a high rank in a board that only contains 12 words, you will need to find more than 45% of them to get an A or higher because of the handicap.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eIf this seems unfair, you'll be pleased to know that the opposite is true for longer boards. Very open boards naturally contain loads of esoteric and rare words that players are not expected to guess. Therefore, a handicap in your favor is applied to your score at the end of the round. The specific handicaps will be visible in your \u003cstrong\u003eScores\u003c/strong\u003e folder breakdown.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eGame Modes\u003c/h2\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-game-modes\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Game Modes\" href=\"#game-modes\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eStandard:\u003c/strong\u003e No penalty whatsoever for guessing incorrect words. \u003cem\u003eRecommended for casual players\u003c/em\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eHardcore:\u003c/strong\u003e If a word you entered is not in the dictionary, at the end of the round, you will be penalized for half of that word's score, including the bonus. So if \u003ccode\u003eSQUADS\u003c/code\u003e was an invalid word, you would be penalized 140 points. \u003cbr\u003e \u003cem\u003eRecommended for competitive players who want to put their vocabulary to the test!\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eIMPORTANT\u003c/strong\u003e: Words that cannot be connected in the board (ie. words that aren't actually formable) do not count as incorrect words, they are simply ignored (except for badge counters, see \u003ca href=\"#badges\"\u003eBadges\u003c/a\u003e). The same applies to 1-and-2 letter words and duplicate entries.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eSpecial Commands (for Hardcore mode only!):\u003c/h3\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-special-commands-for-hardcore-mode-only\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Special Commands (for Hardcore mode only!):\" href=\"#special-commands-for-hardcore-mode-only\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e-WORD\u003c/strong\u003e: Word deletion. Typing \u003ccode\u003e-WORD\u003c/code\u003e will delete an entry from the list. Since Hardcore penalizes for incorrect words, if you made a typo, delete it by typing \u003ccode\u003e-YOURTYPOWORD\u003c/code\u003e in the input box.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e?WORD\u003c/strong\u003e or \u003cstrong\u003eWORD?\u003c/strong\u003e: Word query. Let's say you come across a word you aren't sure is valid. You don't want to risk getting it wrong, but the curiosity is killing you and you want to know if it's a valid word. Simply type \u003ccode\u003e?YOURWORD\u003c/code\u003e or \u003ccode\u003eYOURWORD?\u003c/code\u003e, and at the end of the round, you will be able to check if the word was valid or not, without it affecting your score or badges whatsoever.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cdiv align=\"center\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eGame Sub-Types\u003c/h3\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-game-sub-types\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Game Sub-Types\" .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eQuick Play:\u003c/strong\u003e A completely random board is generated. Simple!\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eWorld Tour:\u003c/strong\u003e Do you have what it takes to slay across all different board types? Go through 10 different boards which range from very closed fast boards to very open long boards! The boards are all still randomly generated, however, you will only play one board of each classification. For example, you will play one extremely short board, one kinda short board, one slightly short board, one average board \u003ccode\u003e...\u003c/code\u003e one extremely open board. The order of these boards is randomized, so pay attention to the background colors so you can react quickly to the fast boards! \u003cbr\u003e\u003cbr\u003e At the end of each round, you will be given a rating and score exactly the same way as in Quick Play, one for each round. At the end of the 10th round, you will see a special end screen with your total score, badges earned and your \u003cstrong\u003eaverage\u003c/strong\u003e rating across all boards! Perhaps some folks are good at short fast words, and others are better at long words and slower play. This game mode balances that since it will test you at 10 different board types!\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cdiv align=\"center\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e*The World Tour summary screen.\u003c/h5\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-the-world-tour-summary-screen\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: *The World Tour summary screen.\" href=\"#the-world-tour-summary-screen\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 src=\"https://private-user-images.githubusercontent.com/177044561/440087089-c30c5e90-b780-4d51-af3a-c98708fa2ff8.png?jwt=eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9.eyJpc3MiOiJnaXRodWIuY29tIiwiYXVkIjoicmF3LmdpdGh1YnVzZXJjb250ZW50LmNvbSIsImtleSI6ImtleTUiLCJleHAiOjE3NDYyNDY0MDEsIm5iZiI6MTc0NjI0NjEwMSwicGF0aCI6Ii8xNzcwNDQ1NjEvNDQwMDg3MDg5LWMzMGM1ZTkwLWI3ODAtNGQ1MS1hZjNhLWM5ODcwOGZhMmZmOC5wbmc_WC1BbXotQWxnb3JpdGhtPUFXUzQtSE1BQy1TSEEyNTYmWC1BbXotQ3JlZGVudGlhbD1BS0lBVkNPRFlMU0E1M1BRSzRaQSUyRjIwMjUwNTAzJTJGdXMtZWFzdC0xJTJGczMlMkZhd3M0X3JlcXVlc3QmWC1BbXotRGF0ZT0yMDI1MDUwM1QwNDIxNDFaJlgtQW16LUV4cGlyZXM9MzAwJlgtQW16LVNpZ25hdHVyZT0xZmVhNjNkZDkwODY2MTVlMGM0ZTNlY2JlODgyNTVkYjQ5ZjVhYmM3MGVjNDZlZjM0YjZjZGI1NWMwZTZjNTcyJlgtQW16LVNpZ25lZEhlYWRlcnM9aG9zdCJ9.wYnWiF436SpPvz0ktJiMkFB4EFuMvyrdnVKc9bMPidE\" style=\"max-width: 100%;\"\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\n\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cbr\u003e\nHere's how to interpret the definition:\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eDefinition 1\u003c/strong\u003e: When you see any word that is preceded by a \u003ccode\u003e=\u003c/code\u003e, it is referring to an alternate spelling or word to refer to the queried word. \u003cbr\u003e In this case, it is telling us that \u003ccode\u003eKRAY\u003c/code\u003e is the same as \u003ccode\u003eKRAI\u003c/code\u003e. But that's not a satisfying answer, is it?\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eDefinition 2\u003c/strong\u003e: The word \u003ccode\u003eKRAI\u003c/code\u003e is automatically searched for your convenience, and we get to the root meaning. An administrative territory in Russia. If any more references are nested, those will be looked up next.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThe \u003ccode\u003en\u003c/code\u003e means the word is a noun. In brackets, you will find how the word is conjugated or pluralized. In this case, it is simply pluralized by adding an S. \u003ccode\u003eKRAYS\u003c/code\u003e and \u003ccode\u003eKRAIS\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThese definitions can iterate a lot in some cases, but hopefully, it is clear enough to get an idea of what the word actually means.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eWTF? Please keep in mind that API services usually have a limited number of uses before you have to pay. For the sake of providing you a completely functional game in this early phase, I have included my own API key built-in since I speculate not a whole bunch of people are going to swarm this game on release.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eIn the future, though, that API key may cease to function and you will be expected to provide your own. Again, the game works completely fine without this function, you don't need to use it. But if you can, show your support for the people who make these APIs by checking out their website and signing up for your own key (they offer free keys as well). fGqKFv"><div class="Box-sc-g0xbh4-0 eoaCFS js-snippet-clipboard-copy-unpositioned undefined" data-hpc="true"><article class="markdown-body entry-content container-lg" itemprop="text"><div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 align="center" tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Woggy</h1><a id="user-content-woggy" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Woggy" href="#woggy"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p align="justify" dir="auto">
  Woggy is basically what Boggle always wanted to be, if only it had been born in the Information Age! Dynamic timer, built-in definitions, and an overhaul to the scoring system that rebalances it in favor of long words!
</p>
<div align="center" dir="auto">

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Installation</h2><a id="user-content-installation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Installation" href="#installation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>If you don't already have Python installed, install it by <a href="https://www.python.org/downloads/" rel="nofollow">visiting here</a>.</li>
<li>Download the <a href="https://github.com/senthenastydynast2/Woggy/archive/refs/heads/main.zip">game .zip file</a>.</li>
<li>Unpack it to a folder of your choice.</li>
<li>Run <code>run.bat</code>.</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">How to Play / Core Mechanics</h2><a id="user-content-how-to-play--core-mechanics" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: How to Play / Core Mechanics" href="#how-to-play--core-mechanics"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">If you don't know how to play Boggle, I suggest you look that up first, since the core gameplay is identical to Boggle. Search for words and type away. Only words 3 letters and up are considered, and you can't go over the same letter twice.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Controls</h3><a id="user-content-controls" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Controls" href="#controls"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Spacebar</strong>: Rotates the board clockwise. This does not alter the current tile distribution, but is very useful in getting a new perspective on the board.</li>
<li><strong>ESC:</strong> Pauses the game. The timer freezes, and tiles go blank until it is unpaused.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Board Generation</h3><a id="user-content-board-generation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Board Generation" href="#board-generation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Depending on your game type, a board will be generated at random (no curated boards here, unlike other Boggle wannabe apps!) based on a probability chance for each letter. The probability of a given letter to appear on the board is the same as that of in a game of Scrabble. For example, out of the 100 tiles in a standard Scrabble game, "E" has 12 tiles, and "Q" has 1. Therefore, E has a 12% chance of appearing in a given tile, and Q has a 1% chance. This creates a natural distribution of letters that would be as similar as possible to a competitive Scrabble game.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Summary Screen</h3><a id="user-content-summary-screen" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Summary Screen" href="#summary-screen"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">At the end of each round, you will be shown a summary of your performance, including your rank letter, round score, badges earned, a list of possible words that you missed (in black) and words that you correctly guessed (in green) with their respective scores:</p>
<div align="center" dir="auto">
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://private-user-images.githubusercontent.com/177044561/440055920-ffb88c3f-f453-4c9d-98af-696d28d762ac.png?jwt=eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9.eyJpc3MiOiJnaXRodWIuY29tIiwiYXVkIjoicmF3LmdpdGh1YnVzZXJjb250ZW50LmNvbSIsImtleSI6ImtleTUiLCJleHAiOjE3NDYyNDY0MDEsIm5iZiI6MTc0NjI0NjEwMSwicGF0aCI6Ii8xNzcwNDQ1NjEvNDQwMDU1OTIwLWZmYjg4YzNmLWY0NTMtNGM5ZC05OGFmLTY5NmQyOGQ3NjJhYy5wbmc_WC1BbXotQWxnb3JpdGhtPUFXUzQtSE1BQy1TSEEyNTYmWC1BbXotQ3JlZGVudGlhbD1BS0lBVkNPRFlMU0E1M1BRSzRaQSUyRjIwMjUwNTAzJTJGdXMtZWFzdC0xJTJGczMlMkZhd3M0X3JlcXVlc3QmWC1BbXotRGF0ZT0yMDI1MDUwM1QwNDIxNDFaJlgtQW16LUV4cGlyZXM9MzAwJlgtQW16LVNpZ25hdHVyZT0yMzZkNDU1NWQzM2RmMWI5N2Y3ZDFmNDdmYjA3OWRmY2U5NDYzYzEyNmZiYzU5YzgyZGIxYzZlYWU1YTRhN2MxJlgtQW16LVNpZ25lZEhlYWRlcnM9aG9zdCJ9.o-kABmPoaWRCJQh0FjzX5duPKovRIj94-JGxUoGyAp0"><img src="https://private-user-images.githubusercontent.com/177044561/440055920-ffb88c3f-f453-4c9d-98af-696d28d762ac.png?jwt=eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9.eyJpc3MiOiJnaXRodWIuY29tIiwiYXVkIjoicmF3LmdpdGh1YnVzZXJjb250ZW50LmNvbSIsImtleSI6ImtleTUiLCJleHAiOjE3NDYyNDY0MDEsIm5iZiI6MTc0NjI0NjEwMSwicGF0aCI6Ii8xNzcwNDQ1NjEvNDQwMDU1OTIwLWZmYjg4YzNmLWY0NTMtNGM5ZC05OGFmLTY5NmQyOGQ3NjJhYy5wbmc_WC1BbXotQWxnb3JpdGhtPUFXUzQtSE1BQy1TSEEyNTYmWC1BbXotQ3JlZGVudGlhbD1BS0lBVkNPRFlMU0E1M1BRSzRaQSUyRjIwMjUwNTAzJTJGdXMtZWFzdC0xJTJGczMlMkZhd3M0X3JlcXVlc3QmWC1BbXotRGF0ZT0yMDI1MDUwM1QwNDIxNDFaJlgtQW16LUV4cGlyZXM9MzAwJlgtQW16LVNpZ25hdHVyZT0yMzZkNDU1NWQzM2RmMWI5N2Y3ZDFmNDdmYjA3OWRmY2U5NDYzYzEyNmZiYzU5YzgyZGIxYzZlYWU1YTRhN2MxJlgtQW16LVNpZ25lZEhlYWRlcnM9aG9zdCJ9.o-kABmPoaWRCJQh0FjzX5duPKovRIj94-JGxUoGyAp0" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
</div>  
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Board Classification (Background Colors)</h3><a id="user-content-board-classification-background-colors" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Board Classification (Background Colors)" href="#board-classification-background-colors"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">What makes Woggy unique to other Boggle clones is its dynamic timer and scoring system. Why would we play for 3:00 minutes on a board that only has 10 words? When you start a board, the total possible score for it is calculated, and a board classification is assigned to it depending on how much potential there is on the board. For very closed boards, the timer is shrunk to as little as 15 seconds and the background turns <strong>red</strong> to indicate a sense of urgency. This type of board will more challenge your speed on finding the few words available. On the other hand, boards with huge score potentials have more exotic background colors, such as sky blue, purple, and green, and feature much longer times (up to 300 seconds!).</p>
<p dir="auto">The background color gives you a hint on how to play: You will want to hurry up on the reddish boards and change your playstyle for more relaxed play on lighter-colored boards.</p>
<p dir="auto">The board's classification nickname is displayed in the End Screen, and it ranges from <code>Impossible Board!</code> all the way to <code>Godlike Board!</code> depending on its potential. There are currently 32 total categories where a board can fit into, each with its own unique timer and scoring parameters.</p>
<div align="center" dir="auto">
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://private-user-images.githubusercontent.com/177044561/440059318-297442e1-6920-482c-bad1-2d836d779447.png?jwt=eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9.eyJpc3MiOiJnaXRodWIuY29tIiwiYXVkIjoicmF3LmdpdGh1YnVzZXJjb250ZW50LmNvbSIsImtleSI6ImtleTUiLCJleHAiOjE3NDYyNDY0MDEsIm5iZiI6MTc0NjI0NjEwMSwicGF0aCI6Ii8xNzcwNDQ1NjEvNDQwMDU5MzE4LTI5NzQ0MmUxLTY5MjAtNDgyYy1iYWQxLTJkODM2ZDc3OTQ0Ny5wbmc_WC1BbXotQWxnb3JpdGhtPUFXUzQtSE1BQy1TSEEyNTYmWC1BbXotQ3JlZGVudGlhbD1BS0lBVkNPRFlMU0E1M1BRSzRaQSUyRjIwMjUwNTAzJTJGdXMtZWFzdC0xJTJGczMlMkZhd3M0X3JlcXVlc3QmWC1BbXotRGF0ZT0yMDI1MDUwM1QwNDIxNDFaJlgtQW16LUV4cGlyZXM9MzAwJlgtQW16LVNpZ25hdHVyZT1iM2ZhN2QzZTExMmUzZWI3Njg2N2RlMGE5Y2JmMDJhOGQ4N2UxOWI0NTAyY2Y2MTM0OWNhNWIzOGYzNGJjMjNlJlgtQW16LVNpZ25lZEhlYWRlcnM9aG9zdCJ9.fCzqP4TeVHyiRE3MO3ZpB0R6ABJAzJ3lw7HWY2Obq5Y"><img src="https://private-user-images.githubusercontent.com/177044561/440059318-297442e1-6920-482c-bad1-2d836d779447.png?jwt=eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9.eyJpc3MiOiJnaXRodWIuY29tIiwiYXVkIjoicmF3LmdpdGh1YnVzZXJjb250ZW50LmNvbSIsImtleSI6ImtleTUiLCJleHAiOjE3NDYyNDY0MDEsIm5iZiI6MTc0NjI0NjEwMSwicGF0aCI6Ii8xNzcwNDQ1NjEvNDQwMDU5MzE4LTI5NzQ0MmUxLTY5MjAtNDgyYy1iYWQxLTJkODM2ZDc3OTQ0Ny5wbmc_WC1BbXotQWxnb3JpdGhtPUFXUzQtSE1BQy1TSEEyNTYmWC1BbXotQ3JlZGVudGlhbD1BS0lBVkNPRFlMU0E1M1BRSzRaQSUyRjIwMjUwNTAzJTJGdXMtZWFzdC0xJTJGczMlMkZhd3M0X3JlcXVlc3QmWC1BbXotRGF0ZT0yMDI1MDUwM1QwNDIxNDFaJlgtQW16LUV4cGlyZXM9MzAwJlgtQW16LVNpZ25hdHVyZT1iM2ZhN2QzZTExMmUzZWI3Njg2N2RlMGE5Y2JmMDJhOGQ4N2UxOWI0NTAyY2Y2MTM0OWNhNWIzOGYzNGJjMjNlJlgtQW16LVNpZ25lZEhlYWRlcnM9aG9zdCJ9.fCzqP4TeVHyiRE3MO3ZpB0R6ABJAzJ3lw7HWY2Obq5Y" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
</div>  
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 align="center" tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">*An example of a board with very high score potential, showing a purplish background to indicate its potential. </h4><a id="user-content-an-example-of-a-board-with-very-high-score-potential-showing-a-purplish-background-to-indicate-its-potential-" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: *An example of a board with very high score potential, showing a purplish background to indicate its potential. <div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Score Logging</h3><a id="user-content-score-logging" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Score Logging" href="#score-logging"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">At the end of each round (or a World Tour game), a text file will be automatically be generated under the <strong>Scores</strong> folder with the date on the title and a breakdown of the entire round. Useful for keeping track of high scores!</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Options</h3><a id="user-content-options" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Options" href="#options"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">-<strong>Tile Size</strong>: This will resize the board tiles for better readability. Please be advised, since the game is still extremely early in development, I haven't yet tested all tile sizes to look good.</p>
<p dir="auto">-<strong>Word Judge</strong>: Turning this off will turn off the comments you get at the end of each round. For those who prefer a judgement-free Woggy experience!</p>
<p dir="auto">All options and latest preferences are automatically saved in <code>Settings\settings.json</code>.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Scoring Rules</h2><a id="user-content-scoring-rules" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Scoring Rules" href="#scoring-rules"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Each tile in Woggy scores the same amount as it does in an official Scrabble board * 10. For example, E = 10, F = 40, Q = 100, etc. In its pure form, the word <code>SQUADS</code> would be worth 160 points.</p>
<p dir="auto">The main difference in scoring is that longer words now have a much higher weight to them due to <strong>score multipliers</strong>. The longer the word, the higher the score multiplier (as opposed to a measly flat bonus the original Boggle grants). This is a great implementation for those who love to seek long words in the board, and it properly compensates players who have the skill required to find them. Here is how much each word is affected by its length:</p>
<div align="center" dir="auto">
<markdown-accessiblity-table><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Word Length</th>
<th>Multiplier</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>3 letters</td>
<td><strong>1x</strong></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>4 letters</td>
<td><strong>1.25x</strong></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>5 letters</td>
<td><strong>1.5x</strong></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>6 letters</td>
<td><strong>1.75x</strong></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>7 letters</td>
<td><strong>2x</strong></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>8 letters</td>
<td><strong>2.5x</strong></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>9 letters</td>
<td><strong>3x</strong></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>10 letters</td>
<td><strong>4x</strong></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>11 letters</td>
<td><strong>5x</strong></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>12 letters</td>
<td><strong>6x</strong></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>13 letters</td>
<td><strong>7x</strong></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>14 letters</td>
<td><strong>8x</strong></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>15 letters</td>
<td><strong>10x</strong></td>
</tr>

<td><strong>12x</strong></td>
</tr>

</table></markdown-accessiblity-table>
</div>
<p dir="auto">With this scoring logic, <code>SQUADS</code> will be worth 280 points, instead of its base 160. While this scoring system might seem a bit overboard, keep in mind that words longer than 9 or 10 are quite rare to find. In the rare occassion that one does exist, one will be properly compensated for finding it.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Rank Determination</h3><a id="user-content-rank-determination" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Rank Determination" href="#rank-determination"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Depending on your performance, you will be shown a rank letter in your end screen. These range from <code>F-</code> all the way to a legendary <code>SS</code>.</p>
<p dir="auto">This score is calculated by several factors, but at its core, it is based on what percentage of the potential score you earned in a given board. For example, only getting a 5% score will net you an <code>F-</code>, but netting 45% will get you a solid <code>A</code>. There are a few more factors to consider, though. "Extreme" boards (very closed or very open) have a handicap to offset scores in an effort to make them more balanced. This means that in order to get a high rank in a board that only contains 12 words, you will need to find more than 45% of them to get an A or higher because of the handicap.</p>
<p dir="auto">If this seems unfair, you'll be pleased to know that the opposite is true for longer boards. Very open boards naturally contain loads of esoteric and rare words that players are not expected to guess. Therefore, a handicap in your favor is applied to your score at the end of the round. The specific handicaps will be visible in your <strong>Scores</strong> folder breakdown.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Game Modes</h2><a id="user-content-game-modes" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Game Modes" href="#game-modes"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Standard:</strong> No penalty whatsoever for guessing incorrect words. <em>Recommended for casual players</em>.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Hardcore:</strong> If a word you entered is not in the dictionary, at the end of the round, you will be penalized for half of that word's score, including the bonus. So if <code>SQUADS</code> was an invalid word, you would be penalized 140 points. <br> <em>Recommended for competitive players who want to put their vocabulary to the test!</em></p>
</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>IMPORTANT</strong>: Words that cannot be connected in the board (ie. words that aren't actually formable) do not count as incorrect words, they are simply ignored (except for badge counters, see <a href="#badges">Badges</a>). The same applies to 1-and-2 letter words and duplicate entries.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Special Commands (for Hardcore mode only!):</h3><a id="user-content-special-commands-for-hardcore-mode-only" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Special Commands (for Hardcore mode only!):" href="#special-commands-for-hardcore-mode-only"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>-WORD</strong>: Word deletion. Typing <code>-WORD</code> will delete an entry from the list. Since Hardcore penalizes for incorrect words, if you made a typo, delete it by typing <code>-YOURTYPOWORD</code> in the input box.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>?WORD</strong> or <strong>WORD?</strong>: Word query. Let's say you come across a word you aren't sure is valid. You don't want to risk getting it wrong, but the curiosity is killing you and you want to know if it's a valid word. Simply type <code>?YOURWORD</code> or <code>YOURWORD?</code>, and at the end of the round, you will be able to check if the word was valid or not, without it affecting your score or badges whatsoever.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div align="center" dir="auto">
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://private-user-images.githubusercontent.com/177044561/440071495-33ffb855-1c8a-4cd4-85bd-4421f9d9af67.png?jwt=eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9.eyJpc3MiOiJnaXRodWIuY29tIiwiYXVkIjoicmF3LmdpdGh1YnVzZXJjb250ZW50LmNvbSIsImtleSI6ImtleTUiLCJleHAiOjE3NDYyNDY0MDEsIm5iZiI6MTc0NjI0NjEwMSwicGF0aCI6Ii8xNzcwNDQ1NjEvNDQwMDcxNDk1LTMzZmZiODU1LTFjOGEtNGNkNC04NWJkLTQ0MjFmOWQ5YWY2Ny5wbmc_WC1BbXotQWxnb3JpdGhtPUFXUzQtSE1BQy1TSEEyNTYmWC1BbXotQ3JlZGVudGlhbD1BS0lBVkNPRFlMU0E1M1BRSzRaQSUyRjIwMjUwNTAzJTJGdXMtZWFzdC0xJTJGczMlMkZhd3M0X3JlcXVlc3QmWC1BbXotRGF0ZT0yMDI1MDUwM1QwNDIxNDFaJlgtQW16LUV4cGlyZXM9MzAwJlgtQW16LVNpZ25hdHVyZT0wZDQ5ZTE5ZWQ3OTk0ODBmMmYwZTkzZDlkNmVjZmFlMDFhZDNjOGEyNDUxODkxNzcyZDM1MWY5NjUzNTk0ZTM1JlgtQW16LVNpZ25lZEhlYWRlcnM9aG9zdCJ9.7FZwT1wI_UCKS5r-R-7deRAd81CVyJxCAywdbRTC0Jo"><img src="https://private-user-images.githubusercontent.com/177044561/440071495-33ffb855-1c8a-4cd4-85bd-4421f9d9af67.png?jwt=eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9.eyJpc3MiOiJnaXRodWIuY29tIiwiYXVkIjoicmF3LmdpdGh1YnVzZXJjb250ZW50LmNvbSIsImtleSI6ImtleTUiLCJleHAiOjE3NDYyNDY0MDEsIm5iZiI6MTc0NjI0NjEwMSwicGF0aCI6Ii8xNzcwNDQ1NjEvNDQwMDcxNDk1LTMzZmZiODU1LTFjOGEtNGNkNC04NWJkLTQ0MjFmOWQ5YWY2Ny5wbmc_WC1BbXotQWxnb3JpdGhtPUFXUzQtSE1BQy1TSEEyNTYmWC1BbXotQ3JlZGVudGlhbD1BS0lBVkNPRFlMU0E1M1BRSzRaQSUyRjIwMjUwNTAzJTJGdXMtZWFzdC0xJTJGczMlMkZhd3M0X3JlcXVlc3QmWC1BbXotRGF0ZT0yMDI1MDUwM1QwNDIxNDFaJlgtQW16LUV4cGlyZXM9MzAwJlgtQW16LVNpZ25hdHVyZT0wZDQ5ZTE5ZWQ3OTk0ODBmMmYwZTkzZDlkNmVjZmFlMDFhZDNjOGEyNDUxODkxNzcyZDM1MWY5NjUzNTk0ZTM1JlgtQW16LVNpZ25lZEhlYWRlcnM9aG9zdCJ9.7FZwT1wI_UCKS5r-R-7deRAd81CVyJxCAywdbRTC0Jo" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
</div>  
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h5 align="center" tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">*In Hardcore mode, if you guessed any words incorrectly or you looked up any words, the buttons above will allow you to see those words. </h5><a id="user-content-in-hardcore-mode-if-you-guessed-any-words-incorrectly-or-you-looked-up-any-words-the-buttons-above-will-allow-you-to-see-those-words-" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: *In Hardcore mode, if you guessed any words incorrectly or you looked up any words, the buttons above will allow you to see those words. " href="#in-hardcore-mode-if-you-guessed-any-words-incorrectly-or-you-looked-up-any-words-the-buttons-above-will-allow-you-to-see-those-words-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Game Sub-Types</h3><a id="user-content-game-sub-types" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Game Sub-Types" href="#game-sub-types"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Quick Play:</strong> A completely random board is generated. Simple!</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>World Tour:</strong> Do you have what it takes to slay across all different board types? Go through 10 different boards which range from very closed fast boards to very open long boards! The boards are all still randomly generated, however, you will only play one board of each classification. For example, you will play one extremely short board, one kinda short board, one slightly short board, one average board <code>...</code> one extremely open board. The order of these boards is randomized, so pay attention to the background colors so you can react quickly to the fast boards! <br><br> At the end of each round, you will be given a rating and score exactly the same way as in Quick Play, one for each round. At the end of the 10th round, you will see a special end screen with your total score, badges earned and your <strong>average</strong> rating across all boards! Perhaps some folks are good at short fast words, and others are better at long words and slower play. This game mode balances that since it will test you at 10 different board types!</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div align="center" dir="auto">
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://private-user-images.githubusercontent.com/177044561/440073600-b6cb9e4e-edfa-4d41-bffa-5c90bc666da5.png?jwt=eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9.eyJpc3MiOiJnaXRodWIuY29tIiwiYXVkIjoicmF3LmdpdGh1YnVzZXJjb250ZW50LmNvbSIsImtleSI6ImtleTUiLCJleHAiOjE3NDYyNDY0MDEsIm5iZiI6MTc0NjI0NjEwMSwicGF0aCI6Ii8xNzcwNDQ1NjEvNDQwMDczNjAwLWI2Y2I5ZTRlLWVkZmEtNGQ0MS1iZmZhLTVjOTBiYzY2NmRhNS5wbmc_WC1BbXotQWxnb3JpdGhtPUFXUzQtSE1BQy1TSEEyNTYmWC1BbXotQ3JlZGVudGlhbD1BS0lBVkNPRFlMU0E1M1BRSzRaQSUyRjIwMjUwNTAzJTJGdXMtZWFzdC0xJTJGczMlMkZhd3M0X3JlcXVlc3QmWC1BbXotRGF0ZT0yMDI1MDUwM1QwNDIxNDFaJlgtQW16LUV4cGlyZXM9MzAwJlgtQW16LVNpZ25hdHVyZT1lMzc2OWY4MTQ2OTE1NzE2YjJjNzNhZjQyODNiNzgwMjlmMDcyYWNlY2U0YzcxNWFiOGYyYTRmOWRiMzZmOTc0JlgtQW16LVNpZ25lZEhlYWRlcnM9aG9zdCJ9.eL3K_4gagIzJdwwkbbbJeOrwqr7e2neHYW_e3BA6_k0"><img src="https://private-user-images.githubusercontent.com/177044561/440073600-b6cb9e4e-edfa-4d41-bffa-5c90bc666da5.png?jwt=eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9.eyJpc3MiOiJnaXRodWIuY29tIiwiYXVkIjoicmF3LmdpdGh1YnVzZXJjb250ZW50LmNvbSIsImtleSI6ImtleTUiLCJleHAiOjE3NDYyNDY0MDEsIm5iZiI6MTc0NjI0NjEwMSwicGF0aCI6Ii8xNzcwNDQ1NjEvNDQwMDczNjAwLWI2Y2I5ZTRlLWVkZmEtNGQ0MS1iZmZhLTVjOTBiYzY2NmRhNS5wbmc_WC1BbXotQWxnb3JpdGhtPUFXUzQtSE1BQy1TSEEyNTYmWC1BbXotQ3JlZGVudGlhbD1BS0lBVkNPRFlMU0E1M1BRSzRaQSUyRjIwMjUwNTAzJTJGdXMtZWFzdC0xJTJGczMlMkZhd3M0X3JlcXVlc3QmWC1BbXotRGF0ZT0yMDI1MDUwM1QwNDIxNDFaJlgtQW16LUV4cGlyZXM9MzAwJlgtQW16LVNpZ25hdHVyZT1lMzc2OWY4MTQ2OTE1NzE2YjJjNzNhZjQyODNiNzgwMjlmMDcyYWNlY2U0YzcxNWFiOGYyYTRmOWRiMzZmOTc0JlgtQW16LVNpZ25lZEhlYWRlcnM9aG9zdCJ9.eL3K_4gagIzJdwwkbbbJeOrwqr7e2neHYW_e3BA6_k0" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
</div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h5 align="center" tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">*The World Tour summary screen.</h5><a id="user-content-the-world-tour-summary-screen" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: *The World Tour summary screen." href="#the-world-tour-summary-screen"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>IMPORTANT</strong>: Board generation for World Tour can be very CPU-intensive, which means hang time might happen during board generation which might be mistaken for a game crash. I plan to optimize the algorithm responsible, but for now, just be patient!</p>

<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Word Monster</strong>: <em>Coming Soon!</em></p>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Badges</h2><a id="user-content-badges" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Badges" href="#badges"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Badges are your secret weapon in achieving higher ranks in your games. When specific criteria is met, your badge is awarded with a popup message at the end of the round letting you know how many (if any) badges you earned, and a specific percentage bonus is applied to your final score (the bonuses stack!):</p>
<div align="center" dir="auto">
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">🏅 Badge List</h3><a id="user-content--badge-list" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 🏅 Badge List" href="#-badge-list"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

      <td><strong>Homerun</strong></td>
      <td>Awarded for guessing a word whose score is equal to the highest scoring word possible.</td>

</div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Definitions</h2><a id="user-content-definitions" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Definitions" href="#definitions"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Dictionary Source</h3><a id="user-content-dictionary-source" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Dictionary Source" href="#dictionary-source"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Before getting into definitions, you may wonder: What makes a valid word valid? Who decides? Why is my favorite WWF word shown as invalid? For which I would have you -- the smart lexicon inquisitor -- take a look at <code>Dictionaries\About_English.txt</code> where I go in an in-depth explanation as to where this dictionary comes from, and why it is the one chosen for this game (as well as for my upcoming Scrabble game!).</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Definition Lookup</h3><a id="user-content-definition-lookup" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Definition Lookup" href="#definition-lookup"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">To look up a definition, simply double-click it. When doing so, you may see something like this:</p>
<div align="center" dir="auto">
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://private-user-images.githubusercontent.com/177044561/440087089-c30c5e90-b780-4d51-af3a-c98708fa2ff8.png?jwt=eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9.eyJpc3MiOiJnaXRodWIuY29tIiwiYXVkIjoicmF3LmdpdGh1YnVzZXJjb250ZW50LmNvbSIsImtleSI6ImtleTUiLCJleHAiOjE3NDYyNDY0MDEsIm5iZiI6MTc0NjI0NjEwMSwicGF0aCI6Ii8xNzcwNDQ1NjEvNDQwMDg3MDg5LWMzMGM1ZTkwLWI3ODAtNGQ1MS1hZjNhLWM5ODcwOGZhMmZmOC5wbmc_WC1BbXotQWxnb3JpdGhtPUFXUzQtSE1BQy1TSEEyNTYmWC1BbXotQ3JlZGVudGlhbD1BS0lBVkNPRFlMU0E1M1BRSzRaQSUyRjIwMjUwNTAzJTJGdXMtZWFzdC0xJTJGczMlMkZhd3M0X3JlcXVlc3QmWC1BbXotRGF0ZT0yMDI1MDUwM1QwNDIxNDFaJlgtQW16LUV4cGlyZXM9MzAwJlgtQW16LVNpZ25hdHVyZT0xZmVhNjNkZDkwODY2MTVlMGM0ZTNlY2JlODgyNTVkYjQ5ZjVhYmM3MGVjNDZlZjM0YjZjZGI1NWMwZTZjNTcyJlgtQW16LVNpZ25lZEhlYWRlcnM9aG9zdCJ9.wYnWiF436SpPvz0ktJiMkFB4EFuMvyrdnVKc9bMPidE"><img src="https://private-user-images.githubusercontent.com/177044561/440087089-c30c5e90-b780-4d51-af3a-c98708fa2ff8.png?jwt=eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9.eyJpc3MiOiJnaXRodWIuY29tIiwiYXVkIjoicmF3LmdpdGh1YnVzZXJjb250ZW50LmNvbSIsImtleSI6ImtleTUiLCJleHAiOjE3NDYyNDY0MDEsIm5iZiI6MTc0NjI0NjEwMSwicGF0aCI6Ii8xNzcwNDQ1NjEvNDQwMDg3MDg5LWMzMGM1ZTkwLWI3ODAtNGQ1MS1hZjNhLWM5ODcwOGZhMmZmOC5wbmc_WC1BbXotQWxnb3JpdGhtPUFXUzQtSE1BQy1TSEEyNTYmWC1BbXotQ3JlZGVudGlhbD1BS0lBVkNPRFlMU0E1M1BRSzRaQSUyRjIwMjUwNTAzJTJGdXMtZWFzdC0xJTJGczMlMkZhd3M0X3JlcXVlc3QmWC1BbXotRGF0ZT0yMDI1MDUwM1QwNDIxNDFaJlgtQW16LUV4cGlyZXM9MzAwJlgtQW16LVNpZ25hdHVyZT0xZmVhNjNkZDkwODY2MTVlMGM0ZTNlY2JlODgyNTVkYjQ5ZjVhYmM3MGVjNDZlZjM0YjZjZGI1NWMwZTZjNTcyJlgtQW16LVNpZ25lZEhlYWRlcnM9aG9zdCJ9.wYnWiF436SpPvz0ktJiMkFB4EFuMvyrdnVKc9bMPidE" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
</div>
<br>
Here's how to interpret the definition:
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Definition 1</strong>: When you see any word that is preceded by a <code>=</code>, it is referring to an alternate spelling or word to refer to the queried word. <br> In this case, it is telling us that <code>KRAY</code> is the same as <code>KRAI</code>. But that's not a satisfying answer, is it?</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Definition 2</strong>: The word <code>KRAI</code> is automatically searched for your convenience, and we get to the root meaning. An administrative territory in Russia. If any more references are nested, those will be looked up next.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">The <code>n</code> means the word is a noun. In brackets, you will find how the word is conjugated or pluralized. In this case, it is simply pluralized by adding an S. <code>KRAYS</code> and <code>KRAIS</code>.</p>
<p dir="auto">These definitions can iterate a lot in some cases, but hopefully, it is clear enough to get an idea of what the word actually means.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">WTF? Button</h3><a id="user-content-wtf-button" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: WTF? Button" href="#wtf-button"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Aaah, the classic scenario: You look up a word, you read the definition, and all you can think of is... WTF?</p>
<p dir="auto">Well, wonder no more! When you press the <code>WTF?</code> button, a Google Images search API will automatically fetch an image of the Word + definition, in an attempt to illustrate what the mysterious word actually is. Like this:</p>
<div align="center" dir="auto">
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://private-user-images.githubusercontent.com/177044561/440087817-95ab5e7e-4c5d-43ba-8a5a-883d8a01d2c1.png?jwt=eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9.eyJpc3MiOiJnaXRodWIuY29tIiwiYXVkIjoicmF3LmdpdGh1YnVzZXJjb250ZW50LmNvbSIsImtleSI6ImtleTUiLCJleHAiOjE3NDYyNDY0MDEsIm5iZiI6MTc0NjI0NjEwMSwicGF0aCI6Ii8xNzcwNDQ1NjEvNDQwMDg3ODE3LTk1YWI1ZTdlLTRjNWQtNDNiYS04YTVhLTg4M2Q4YTAxZDJjMS5wbmc_WC1BbXotQWxnb3JpdGhtPUFXUzQtSE1BQy1TSEEyNTYmWC1BbXotQ3JlZGVudGlhbD1BS0lBVkNPRFlMU0E1M1BRSzRaQSUyRjIwMjUwNTAzJTJGdXMtZWFzdC0xJTJGczMlMkZhd3M0X3JlcXVlc3QmWC1BbXotRGF0ZT0yMDI1MDUwM1QwNDIxNDFaJlgtQW16LUV4cGlyZXM9MzAwJlgtQW16LVNpZ25hdHVyZT1jMzY5NTcyODYwOWY4OTZmMDI4MjU0MTM4MzBiNDgyNDQwOGIyNGZlYjcxZDE1ZWY4NTIyZTY1ZmFiYjc1NDUzJlgtQW16LVNpZ25lZEhlYWRlcnM9aG9zdCJ9.PTb_fAMTnHTunOuIAFP-Enc251R10ANxCwXQZy6EuZw"><img src="https://private-user-images.githubusercontent.com/177044561/440087817-95ab5e7e-4c5d-43ba-8a5a-883d8a01d2c1.png?jwt=eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9.eyJpc3MiOiJnaXRodWIuY29tIiwiYXVkIjoicmF3LmdpdGh1YnVzZXJjb250ZW50LmNvbSIsImtleSI6ImtleTUiLCJleHAiOjE3NDYyNDY0MDEsIm5iZiI6MTc0NjI0NjEwMSwicGF0aCI6Ii8xNzcwNDQ1NjEvNDQwMDg3ODE3LTk1YWI1ZTdlLTRjNWQtNDNiYS04YTVhLTg4M2Q4YTAxZDJjMS5wbmc_WC1BbXotQWxnb3JpdGhtPUFXUzQtSE1BQy1TSEEyNTYmWC1BbXotQ3JlZGVudGlhbD1BS0lBVkNPRFlMU0E1M1BRSzRaQSUyRjIwMjUwNTAzJTJGdXMtZWFzdC0xJTJGczMlMkZhd3M0X3JlcXVlc3QmWC1BbXotRGF0ZT0yMDI1MDUwM1QwNDIxNDFaJlgtQW16LUV4cGlyZXM9MzAwJlgtQW16LVNpZ25hdHVyZT1jMzY5NTcyODYwOWY4OTZmMDI4MjU0MTM4MzBiNDgyNDQwOGIyNGZlYjcxZDE1ZWY4NTIyZTY1ZmFiYjc1NDUzJlgtQW16LVNpZ25lZEhlYWRlcnM9aG9zdCJ9.PTb_fAMTnHTunOuIAFP-Enc251R10ANxCwXQZy6EuZw" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
</div>
<p dir="auto">This completely optional and convenient service is provided using a free API from a website called <a href="https://www.scrapingdog.com/" rel="nofollow">Scraping Dog</a>. Please keep in mind that API services usually have a limited number of uses before you have to pay. For the sake of providing you a completely functional game in this early phase, I have included my own API key built-in since I speculate not a whole bunch of people are going to swarm this game on release.</p>
<p dir="auto">In the future, though, that API key may cease to function and you will be expected to provide your own. Again, the game works completely fine without this function, you don't need to use it. But if you can, show your support for the people who make these APIs by checking out their website and signing up for your own key (they offer free keys as well). Once you do get your own API key, you can replace the one found in <code>utils.py</code>, simply open the file with any text editor and replace the API key in line 18.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Coming Soon</h2><a id="user-content-coming-soon" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Coming Soon" href="#coming-soon"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
